  <script type="text/javascript">
    (function() {
        var contextPath = '/jira';
        var eventBuffer = [];

        function printDeprecatedMsg() {
            if (console && console.warn) {
                console.warn('DEPRECATED JS - contextPath global variable has been deprecated since 7.4.0. Use `wrm/context-path` module instead.');
            }
        }

        function sendEvent(analytics, postfix) {
            analytics.send({
                name: 'js.globals.contextPath.' + postfix
            });
        }

        function sendDeprecatedEvent(postfix) {
            try {
                var analytics = require('jira/analytics');
                if (eventBuffer.length) {
                    eventBuffer.forEach(function(value) {
                        sendEvent(analytics, value);
                    });
                    eventBuffer = [];
                }

                if (postfix) {
                    sendEvent(analytics, postfix);
                }
            } catch(ex) {
                eventBuffer.push(postfix);
                setTimeout(sendDeprecatedEvent, 1000);
            }
        }

        Object.defineProperty(window, 'contextPath', {
            get: function() {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('get');
                return contextPath;
            },
            set: function(value) {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('set');
                contextPath = value;
            }
        });
    })();

</script>

                <h2 class="toggle-title">Description</h2>
               </div>
               <div class="mod-content">
                <div id="description-val" class="field-ignore-highlight"> 
                 <div class="user-content-block"> 
                  <p>JFlex (<a href="http://www.jflex.de/" class="external-link" rel="nofollow">http://www.jflex.de/</a>) can be used to generate a faster (up to several times) replacement for StandardAnalyzer. Will add a patch and a simple benchmark code in a while.</p>

Take the following &gt;text: \\n&gt; \\n&gt;78academyawards\\/rules\\/rule02.html,7194,7227,type \\n&gt; \\n&gt;which was tokenized by the original StandardAnalyzer as one &lt;NUM&gt;. If you look at the definition of the &lt;NUM&gt; token: \\n&gt; \\n&gt;\\/\\/ every other segment must have at least one digit \\n&gt;&lt;NUM: (&lt;ALPHANUM&gt; &lt;P&gt; &lt;HAS_DIGIT&gt; \\n&gt;       | &lt;HAS_DIGIT&gt; &lt;P&gt; &lt;ALPHANUM&gt; \\n&gt;       | &lt;ALPHANUM&gt; (&lt;P&gt; &lt;HAS_DIGIT&gt; &lt;P&gt; &lt;ALPHANUM&gt;)+ \\n&gt;       | &lt;HAS_DIGIT&gt; (&lt;P&gt; &lt;ALPHANUM&gt; &lt;P&gt; &lt;HAS_DIGIT&gt;)+ \\n&gt;       | &lt;ALPHANUM&gt; &lt;P&gt; &lt;HAS_DIGIT&gt; (&lt;P&gt; &lt;ALPHANUM&gt; &lt;P&gt; &lt;HAS_DIGIT&gt;)+ \\n&gt;       | &lt;HAS_DIGIT&gt; &lt;P&gt; &lt;ALPHANUM&gt; (&lt;P&gt; &lt;HAS_DIGIT&gt; &lt;P&gt; &lt;ALPHANUM&gt;)+ \\n&gt;        ) \\n&gt; \\n&gt;you\'ll see that, as explained in the comment, every other segment must have at least one digit. But actually, according to my understanding, this &gt;rule should not match the above text as a whole (and with JFlex it doesn\'t , actually). Below is the text split by punctuation characters, and it looks &gt;like there is no way of splitting this text into alternating segments, every second of which must have a digit (A = ALPHANUM, H = HAS_DIGIT): \\n&gt; \\n&gt;78academyawards \\/ rules \\/ rule02 . html , 7194 , 7227 , type \\n&gt;                H P A P H P A P H P A P H?* (starting from the beginning) \\n&gt;                                                                              H?* P A P H P A (starting from the end) \\n&gt; \\n&gt;* (would have to be H, but no digits in substring \\\"type\\\" or \\\"html\\\") \\n&gt; \\n&gt;I have no idea why JavaCC matched the whole text as a &lt;NUM&gt;, JFlex behaved \\\"more correctly\\\" here.  \\n\\n I think that JavaCC is correct here. Every other segment must have a digit: 78academyawards \\/ rules \\/ rule02 . html  \\nIt looks to me like every other segment does have a digit. First segment has a digit, second does not, third does, fourth does not. Matches NUM correctly.              \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n\u003c\\/div\u003e\\n                             \\n\\n\\n\u003cdiv id=\\\"comment-12517371\\\" class=\\\"issue-data-block activity-comment twixi-block  expanded\\\"\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap verbose actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Collapse comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-expanded\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eHide\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-links\\\"\u003e\\n                \u003ca href=\\\"\\/jira\\/browse\\/LUCENE-966?focusedCommentId=12517371&page=com.atlassian.jira.plugin.system.issuetabpanels:comment-tabpanel#comment-12517371\\\"\\n                   title=\\\"Right click and copy link for a permanent link to this comment.\\\" class=\\\"activitymodule-link issue-comment-action\\\"\u003e\\n                    \u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-link\\\"\u003ePermalink\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n                                            \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details\\\"\u003e        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"stanislaw.osinski\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_12517371_verbose\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=stanislaw.osinski\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"stanislaw.osinski\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Stanislaw Osinski\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  -
